***зарок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зарок.html>заро́к</a> (29162)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zarokъ</i>. Deverbal from early <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zarekti</i> (later <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zareťi</i>), with <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Indo-European_ablaut" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Indo-European ablaut">Indo-European ablaut</a> typical of nouns. Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">заре́чь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaréčʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to prohibit, to force to renounce</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">заре́чься</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaréčʹsja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to renounce, to forswear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарок.html>заро́к</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarók</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарок.html>заро́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарок.html>заро́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарок.html>заро́ков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>negative oath or vow <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">solemn promise not to do something</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарубежье.html>зарубе́жье</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarubéžʹje</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарубежье.html>зарубе́жья</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарубежье.html>зарубе́жья</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарубежье.html>зарубе́жий</a></b>)

***зарубить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зарубить.html>заруби́ть</a> (12710)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубить.html>руби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарубить.html>заруби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarubítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заруба́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to kill with a sabre <i>[axe, etc]</i></li>
<li>to notch, to make an incision <i>(on)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:зарубить.html>заруби́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себе́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нос.html>носу</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zarubí</b> éto sebé na nosu</i> ― <span class="e-translation"> mark my words; put that in your pipe and smoke it; don't you forget it</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mining</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to hew, to make a cut <i>(in)</i></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to ruin, to turn down, to say no <i>(to)</i>, to shoot down <i>(in flames)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарубка.html>зару́бка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zarúbka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубить.html>руби́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубка.html>ру́бка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rúbka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рубанок.html>руба́нок</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rubánok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ру́бище</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rúbišče</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***зарывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зарывать.html>зарыва́ть</a> (19040)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарыть.html>зары́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zarýtʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарывать.html>зарыва́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaryvátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарыть.html>зары́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bury
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:зарывать.html>зарыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>зе́млю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaryvátʹ</b> talánt v zémlju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to let one's talent go to waste</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to <b>bury</b> (one's) talent in the earth</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fill up <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with earth</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to make (a ditch, pit, etc.) level with the ground
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:зарывать.html>зарыва́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:канава.html>кана́ву</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaryvátʹ</b> kanávu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fill up/in a ditch</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарывать.html>зарыва́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zaryvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зарыть.html>зары́ть</a> (9073)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рыть.html>рыть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rytʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарыть.html>зары́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarýtʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарывать.html>зарыва́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bury
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:зарыть.html>зары́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:талант.html>тала́нт</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:земля.html>зе́млю</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zarýtʹ</b> talánt v zémlju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to let one's talent go to waste</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">to <b>bury</b> (one's) talent in the earth</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вот.html>вот</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:где.html>где</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:собака.html>соба́ка</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зарытый.html>зары́та</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vot gde sobáka <b>zarýta</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">so that's where the problem lies!; that's where the shoe pinches</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">here's where the dog is <b>buried</b></span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to fill up <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">with earth</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to make (a ditch, pit, etc.) level with the ground
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:зарыть.html>зары́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:канава.html>кана́ву</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zarýtʹ</b> kanávu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to fill up/in a ditch</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закопать.html>закопа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zakopátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***заря.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заря.html>заря́</a> (4470)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*zorja</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заря.html>заря́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarjá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заря.html>зари́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заря.html>зо́ри</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заря.html>зорь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>dawn, daybreak
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заря.html>заре́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>zaré</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">at the earliest stage, at the beginning</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">at the <b>dawn</b></span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заря.html>зари́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заря.html>зари́</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ot <b>zarí</b> do <b>zarí</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from morning to night, from dawn to dusk</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally">from <b>dawn</b> to <b>dawn</b></span>”)</div></dd></dl></li>
<li>dusk, nightfall</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> reveille</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tattoo, retreat</li>
<li>outset, start</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарница.html>зарни́ца</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zarníca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заря́нка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zarjánka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озарять.html>озаря́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ozarjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озарить.html>озари́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ozarítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заряд.html>заря́д</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarjád</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заряд.html>заря́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заряд.html>заря́ды</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заряд.html>заря́дов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>charge, a load of explosive</li>
<li>shot, shell</li>
<li>quantity of electricity</li>
<li>electrically charged body</li>
<li>conserved quantum number</li>
<li>store, fund, supply</li>
<li>charging up</li>
<li>snow squall</li></ol>

***зарядить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зарядить.html>заряди́ть</a> (8837)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарядить.html>заряди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarjadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заряжать.html>заряжа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to load (a weapon)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:взять.html>возьми́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пистолет.html>пистоле́т</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зарядить.html>заряди́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стрелять.html>стреля́й</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vozʹmí pistolét, <b>zarjadí</b> i streljáj.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Take the gun, load and shoot.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to charge (a battery, accumulator, etc.)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:забыть.html>забу́дь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зарядить.html>заряди́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:телефон.html>телефо́н</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne zabúdʹ <b>zarjadítʹ</b> telefón.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Don't forget to charge the (mobile) phone.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to inspire, to imbue</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заряд.html>заря́д</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zarjád</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарядка.html>заря́дка</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zarjádka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заряженный.html>заря́женный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zarjážennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарядить.html>заряди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarjadítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заряжать.html>заряжа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">folk  colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep repeating (an action) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">+ accusative or infinitive</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>Он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:зарядить.html>заряди́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гость.html>го́сти</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">On <b>zarjadíl</b> xodítʹ v gósti.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He got into a habit of going to visit (friends, relatives)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to fall nonstop <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of rain</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>

***зарядный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:зарядный.html>заря́дный</a> (20910)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заряд.html>заря́д</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zarjád</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарядный.html>заря́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarjádnyj</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заряжавший.html>заряжа́вший</a> (9883)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заряжать.html>заряжа́ть</a> (9883)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарядить.html>заряди́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zarjadítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заряжать.html>заряжа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zarjažátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:зарядить.html>заряди́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to load <i>(weapon)</i></li>
<li>to charge <i>(battery)</i></li>
<li>to inspire, to imbue</li></ol>
